Téléchargez et ouvrez des dessins 2D au format DWG directement à partir du disque dur, d'un e-mail ou d'un dispositif stockage externe et affichez tous les aspects de votre fichier DWG, notamment les références externes, les calques et les calques d'image sous-jacents. Mettez à niveau vers AutoCAD mobile Premium pour activer des outils de modification et de dessin. Que vous travailliez en ligne ou hors ligne, au bureau ou sur le terrain, vous pouvez reproduire chaque détail, où que vous soyez. \r\n\r\nQue vous souhaitiez dessiner, visualiser ou annoter un fichier DWG, AutoCAD mobile a l'offre qui vous convient. \r\n\r\nFonctions :\r\n\r\n• Version Premium d'évaluation gratuite pour les nouveaux utilisateurs sans aucune obligation\r\n• Ouvrez et affichez vos fichiers DWG\r\n• Mesurez avec précision tout en étant sur le site\r\n• Utilisez les fonctions Panoramique et Zoom multi-tactiles pour vous déplacer facilement dans de grands dessins\r\n• Travaillez hors ligne et synchronisez vos modifications lors de votre reconnexion\r\n• Connectivité au stockage externe sur le cloud - visualisation des dessins depuis Google Drive, Dropbox, OneDrive, etc.\r\n• Partagez vos conceptions avec d'autres utilisateurs, directement depuis votre mobile \r\n• Tracez des conceptions au format PDF et partagez-les par e-mail\r\n• Téléchargez des conceptions au avancée \r\n• Afficher et modifier des propriétés d'objets\r\n• Une palette de blocs contenant tous les blocs du dessin, pour permettre à l'utilisateur d'insérer des blocs\r\n• Outils de dessin Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it. The test also requires about 4x the memory. Therefore R15 and R20 results cannot be compared.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 and Cinema 4D R20 incorporate the latest rendering architectures, including integration of Intel’s Embree raytracing technology and advanced features on modern CPUs from AMD and Intel that allow users to render the same scene on the same hardware twice as fast as previously. \r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 provides improved benchmark accuracy for current and next generation CPUs to test if a machine runs stable on a high CPU load, if the cooling solution of a desktop or notebook is sufficient for longer running tasks to deliver the full potential of the CPU, and if a machine is able to handle demanding real-life 3D tasks.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 does not test GPU performance.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 will not launch on unsupported processors. On systems lacking sufficient RAM to load the test scene, a warning will be displayed and the CPU benchmark will not be executed.\r\n\r\n•\tBackground tasks can significantly influence measurement and create diverse results. It's always a good idea to shut down all running programs and disable any virus checking or disk indexing, but it's impossible to eliminate all background processes. Modern operating systems perform various background tasks that cannot or should not be disabled, even though they could have a minor influence on the results.\r\n\r\n•\tTest results can vary slightly because it's impossible to disable every background task of the operating system. These tasks are one factor that may have a slight influence on measurements. Also, modern computers and graphics cards dynamically adjust clock speeds based on environmental conditions like power and temperature. For instance, processors will reduce clock speed when running too hot to allow for cooling and prevent damage. With many modern processors the reverse is also true. They are able to overclock themselves when the temperature is low enough. So, a system freshly started in a relatively cool environment will typically run faster than the same system that has been performing benchmarks for several hours in a heated office.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NBLGGH4RFHK","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"AdBlock","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.64693.13510798887413064.7dec4a64-65c8-45c3-96b8-8f8f9b2600a0.d2f3940c-9467-43d9-9cc5-448ef5148c5b","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"white","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Gratuit","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["BetaFish.AdBlock_c1wakc4j0nefm"],"ContentIds":["e56f1d49-7ed1-85c0-f549-2914e47e34b2"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"AdBlock.
